[USER]
im going to share and instructions plan for applying some files to to be pushe to my git repo in agent mode. can you do this?

[ASSISTANT]
Yep—drop the plan and the files. I can sanity-check your steps, map the files into the repo, and spit out a one-shot script (or PR) that does the whole dance without hand-waving.

Here’s a sane default “agent-ish” flow you can use as-is. It clones clean, creates a feature branch, copies your files in, commits, pushes, and (optionally) opens a PR via `gh` if it’s available.

```bash
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# ==== CONFIG (edit or pass as env vars) ====
: "${REPO_URL:?Set REPO_URL (e.g. git@github.com:user/repo.git)}"
: "${SRC_PATH:?Set SRC_PATH to the folder/zip with files to apply}"
BASE_BRANCH="${BASE_BRANCH:-main}"
NEW_BRANCH="${NEW_BRANCH:-feature/apply-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)}"
DEST_SUBDIR="${DEST_SUBDIR:-.}"              # where inside repo to place files
COMMIT_MSG="${COMMIT_MSG:-Apply files}"
GIT_NAME="${GIT_NAME:-}"
GIT_EMAIL="${GIT_EMAIL:-}"
OPEN_PR="${OPEN_PR:-true}"                   # requires GitHub CLI `gh`
EXCLUDES_FILE="${EXCLUDES_FILE:-}"           # optional path to rsync --exclude-from list
DRY_RUN="${DRY_RUN:-false}"                  # true -> show changes, don’t push

# ==== Prep ====
tmpdir="$(mktemp -d)"; trap 'rm -rf "$tmpdir"' EXIT
echo "Working in $tmpdir"

# Support zip or directory
worksrc="$tmpdir/src"
mkdir -p "$worksrc"
if [[ -f "$SRC_PATH" && "$SRC_PATH" == *.zip ]]; then
  unzip -q "$SRC_PATH" -d "$worksrc"
elif [[ -d "$SRC_PATH" ]]; then
  rsync -a "$SRC_PATH"/ "$worksrc"/
else
  echo "SRC_PATH must be a dir or .zip"; exit 2
fi

# ==== Clone and branch ====
git clone --depth 1 --branch "$BASE_BRANCH" "$REPO_URL" "$tmpdir/repo"
cd "$tmpdir/repo"
git checkout -b "$NEW_BRANCH"

# ==== Copy files into repo ====
mkdir -p "$DEST_SUBDIR"
rsync -a \
  ${EXCLUDES_FILE:+--exclude-from "$EXCLUDES_FILE"} \
  "$worksrc"/ "$DEST_SUBDIR"/

# ==== Show diff (optional dry run) ====
echo "Staging changes…"
git add -A
if git diff --cached --quiet; then
  echo "No changes to commit. Exiting."
  exit 0
fi

echo "Pending changes:"
git status --short
git diff --cached --stat

if [[ "$DRY_RUN" == "true" ]]; then
  echo "DRY_RUN=true — not committing/pushing."; exit 0
fi

# ==== Commit & push ====
[[ -n "$GIT_NAME" ]] && git config user.name "$GIT_NAME"
[[ -n "$GIT_EMAIL" ]] && git config user.email "$GIT_EMAIL"

git commit -m "$COMMIT_MSG"
git push -u origin "$NEW_BRANCH"

# ==== Open PR (optional) ====
if [[ "$OPEN_PR" == "true" ]] && command -v gh >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  gh pr create -B "$BASE_BRANCH" -t "$COMMIT_MSG" -b "Automated file apply"
  echo "PR opened."
else
  echo "PR not opened (either OPEN_PR=false or gh not installed)."
fi

echo "Done. Branch: $NEW_BRANCH"
```

How I’ll run this with your stuff:
- You give me the plan and the files (zip or folder).  
- I’ll map source → destination paths, write the exact config block, and add any exclude patterns you need.  
- If you want it fully “agent mode,” I’ll convert this into a watcher (inotify) that auto-commits on changes, or a GitHub Action that applies a known package into the repo on demand.

Defaults I’ll enforce unless you say otherwise:
- Base branch `main`, feature branch `feature/apply-<timestamp>`.
- No destructive deletes (`rsync` won’t nuke existing files unless you ask for `--delete`).
- PR created if `gh` is present; otherwise you get a pushed branch ready for review.
- Clean clone every time, so we don’t stomp local work.

When you’re ready, toss in the plan + files and any must-haves (target repo URL, base branch, where inside the repo they should land, commit message style, and whether you want a PR). I’ll wire it up and hand you your customized, push-ready script.

## 1. Overview of Necessary Updates

My analysis of your repository reveals that several key files contain outdated and incorrect novella titles. To ensure the integrity of your OmniMeta Space, the following files and directories must be updated:

1.  **Bible Placeholder Files:** All 30 placeholder files in `04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles/` have incorrect titles and need to be renamed.
2.  **Master Timeline:** The `01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md` file in `03_Structural_Timelines/` uses the old, incorrect titles.
3.  **Story Spine Mapping:** The `09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md` file in `03_Structural_Timelines/` also uses the old, incorrect titles.
4.  **Prose Engine Prompts:** The prompts in `04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES/` likely reference the old titles and will need to be updated.

---

## 2. Step-by-Step Integration Instructions

# Create a push-ready script and inspect the uploaded ZIP to summarize what's inside.
import os, zipfile, re, textwrap, json, pathlib

zip_path = "/mnt/data/corrected_omnimeta_files.zip"

summary = {"zip_exists": os.path.exists(zip_path), "bible_files_found": [], "bibles_present_numbers": [], "bibles_missing_numbers": []}

if os.path.exists(zip_path):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path) as z:
        names = z.namelist()
        bible_files = [n for n in names if re.search(r"/N\d{2}_Bible_.*\.md$", n)]
        summary["bible_files_found"] = bible_files
        nums = sorted(set(int(re.search(r"N(\d{2})", n).group(1)) for n in bible_files))
        summary["bibles_present_numbers"] = nums
        summary["bibles_missing_numbers"] = [i for i in range(1,31) if i not in nums]

script = r"""#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# ===== OmniMeta "agent mode" apply =====
# This script:
#  - Clones your repo fresh on a feature branch
#  - Applies corrected Bible files from a ZIP
#  - Renames N28/N29 to the corrected titles
#  - Updates titles in timeline + story-spine + prose engines
#  - Commits, pushes, and (optionally) opens a PR

# ========== CONFIG (edit or pass as env) ==========
: "${REPO_URL:?Set REPO_URL, e.g. git@github.com:user/omnimeta-saga-universe.git}"
BASE_BRANCH="${BASE_BRANCH:-main}"
NEW_BRANCH="${NEW_BRANCH:-chore/omnimeta-apply-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)}"
ZIP_PATH="${ZIP_PATH:-./corrected_omnimeta_files.zip}"  # path to your uploaded ZIP
OPEN_PR="${OPEN_PR:-true}"                               # requires GitHub CLI `gh`
DRY_RUN="${DRY_RUN:-false}"
GIT_NAME="${GIT_NAME:-}"
GIT_EMAIL="${GIT_EMAIL:-}"

# Repo-relative paths to touch
BIBLES_DIR="04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles"
TIMELINE_FILE="03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md"
STORY_SPINE_FILE="03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md"
PROSE_DIR="04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES"

# Corrected titles for late BREAK turn
TITLE_N28="Echoes End"
TITLE_N29="Apex of Stasis"

# ===== Prep temp =====
tmpdir="$(mktemp -d)"; trap 'rm -rf \"$tmpdir\"' EXIT
echo "Working in $tmpdir"

# ===== Unpack ZIP =====
if [[ ! -f "$ZIP_PATH" ]]; then
  echo "ZIP_PATH not found: $ZIP_PATH" >&2; exit 2
fi

unzip -q "$ZIP_PATH" -d "$tmpdir/src"
# Pick a directory that actually contains the files
srcroot=""
if compgen -G "$tmpdir/src/*/N??_Bible_*.md" > /dev/null; then
  # First subdir containing Bible md files
  srcroot="$(dirname "$(ls "$tmpdir"/src/*/N??_Bible_*.md | head -n1)")"
else
  # Maybe they sit at the root
  if compgen -G "$tmpdir/src/N??_Bible_*.md" > /dev/null; then
    srcroot="$tmpdir/src"
  fi
fi

if [[ -z "$srcroot" ]]; then
  echo "No N??_Bible_*.md files found in ZIP. Nothing to apply." >&2; exit 3
fi

echo "Source root: $srcroot"

# ===== Clone repo and branch =====
git clone --depth 1 --branch "$BASE_BRANCH" "$REPO_URL" "$tmpdir/repo"
cd "$tmpdir/repo"
git checkout -b "$NEW_BRANCH"

echo "Found $have_count Bible files in ZIP."

if [[ "$have_count" -eq 30 ]]; then

  rm -f "$BIBLES_DIR"/N??_Bible_*.md || true

  echo "Partial set detected — WILL NOT delete existing files."

python3 - <<'PY'
import os, re, sys, json, pathlib

repo = pathlib.Path(".")
timeline = repo / os.environ.get("TIMELINE_FILE", "03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md")
spine = repo / os.environ.get("STORY_SPINE_FILE", "03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md")
prose_dir = repo / os.environ.get("PROSE_DIR", "04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES")

# Corrections
fixes = {
    "All Constructs Fall": os.environ.get("TITLE_N28","Echoes End"),
    "Knotted Resolution": os.environ.get("TITLE_N29","Apex of Stasis"),
}

def safe_replace_file(path, replacements):
    if not path.exists(): 
        print(f"[skip] {path} (not found)")
        return 0
    text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    count = 0
    for old, new in replacements.items():
        text, n = re.subn(rf'\\b{re.escape(old)}\\b', new, text)
        count += n
    # Also fix table rows like: | N28 | E | something |
    def fix_row(m):
        n = m.group("n")
        t = m.group("title")
        new_title = fixes["All Constructs Fall"] if n == "28" else fixes["Knotted Resolution"]
        return f"{m.group('pre')}| N{n} | {m.group('acro')} | {new_title} |"
    text = re.sub(r'(?P<pre>^\\s*\\|\\s*)N(?P<n>28|29)\\s*\\|\\s*(?P<acro>[A-Z])\\s*\\|\\s*(?P<title)[^|]+\\|',
                  fix_row, text, flags=re.M)
    path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")
    print(f"[fix] {path} -> {count} plain replacements + table normalization")
    return count

total = 0
total += safe_replace_file(timeline, fixes)
total += safe_replace_file(spine, fixes)

# Sweep prose engines for the old titles
def grep_paths(root):
    for p in root.rglob("*"):
        if p.is_file() and p.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml", ".json"}:
            yield p

eng_repls = 0
for p in (list(grep_paths(prose_dir)) if prose_dir.exists() else []):
    txt = p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    new = txt
    for old, newtitle in fixes.items():
        new = re.sub(rf'\\b{re.escape(old)}\\b', newtitle, new)
    if new != txt:
        p.write_text(new, encoding="utf-8")
        eng_repls += 1
        print(f"[fix] {p} (updated old titles)")
print(f"[summary] timeline/spine replacements: {total}, prose files updated: {eng_repls}")
PY

echo "Staging changes…"
git add -A

if git diff --cached --quiet; then
  echo "No changes to commit."
  exit 0
fi

if [[ -n "$GIT_NAME" ]]; then git config user.name "$GIT_NAME"; fi
if [[ -n "$GIT_EMAIL" ]]; then git config user.email "$GIT_EMAIL"; fi

if [[ "$DRY_RUN" == "true" ]]; then
  echo "DRY_RUN=true — showing diff only:"
  git status --short
  git diff --cached --stat
  exit 0
fi

COMMIT_MSG="Apply corrected OmniMeta files: bibles + title fixes (N28→\"$TITLE_N28\", N29→\"$TITLE_N29\")"
git commit -m "$COMMIT_MSG"

if [[ "$OPEN_PR" == "true" ]] && command -v gh >/dev/null 2>&1; then

fi

your plan called for “delete all 30” and the specific renames (N28→Echoes End, N29→Apex of Stasis); i’ve honored the renames and made the “delete all 30” conditional so you don’t lose half your set when only 15 are present. fileciteturn2file0L26-L30

## what the script does (agent-y and idempotent)
- fresh clone on a feature branch  
- apply bible files from the zip; **only deletes all placeholders if it finds all 30**; otherwise it overlays what’s present and logs what’s missing  
- renames N28/N29 to the corrected titles  
- normalizes titles in:
  - `03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md`
  - `03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md`  
  and sweeps `04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES/` for any remaining old N28/N29 references, replacing them in-place (safe, text-only). fileciteturn2file0L32-L46
- commits, pushes, and optionally opens a PR (uses `gh` if present)

the corrected late-BREAK titles baked in:
- **N28:** Echoes End  
- **N29:** Apex of Stasis**.** fileciteturn2file0L91-L92

## notes / gotchas (the “don’t shoot your own foot” section)
- if you truly want the “delete all 30, then replace” behavior, make sure the zip contains **all 30** `N##_Bible_*.md` files. with the current zip (N16–N30 only), the script will **not** delete first; it will overlay and rename N28/N29 safely. fileciteturn2file0L26-L30
- timeline + spine fixes only change the late-titles (N28/N29) and table rows if present; they won’t touch unrelated prose. fileciteturn2file0L32-L46

# Create an on-repo audit script that the user can run locally to generate a Markdown report.
from pathlib import Path

audit_script = r'''#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
OmniMeta repo audit — checks title normalization & file layout.

Usage:
  python3 omnimeta_repo_audit.py /path/to/your/repo  [--write]

If --write is passed, the report files will be written into the repo root as:
  - omnimeta_audit_report.md
  - omnimeta_audit_summary.json
Otherwise, results are printed to stdout.

What it checks:
  1) 30 Bible files present and uniquely numbered (N01..N30)
  2) N28/N29 titles propagated: "Echoes End" / "Apex of Stasis"
     and the old titles ("All Constructs Fall" / "Knotted Resolution") are absent
  3) Timeline & Story-Spine contain the corrected titles
  4) Prose engines contain no references to old titles
  5) Optional: the last 15 commits that touched relevant files/directories (if git is available)
"""

import sys, os, re, json, subprocess, textwrap
from pathlib import Path
from collections import defaultdict

CORRECT_TITLES = {
    28: "Echoes End",
    29: "Apex of Stasis",
}
OLD_TITLES = {
    28: "All Constructs Fall",
    29: "Knotted Resolution",
}

# Repo structure of interest
BIBLES_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles")
TIMELINE = Path("03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md")
STORY_SPINE = Path("03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md")
PROSE_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES")

MD_HEADER = "# OmniMeta Repository Audit Report\n"

def find_repo_root(arg_path: Path) -> Path:
    rp = arg_path.resolve()
    if (rp / ".git").exists() or (rp / BIBLES_DIR).exists():
        return rp
    # walk upwards a few levels, just in case the user passed a subdir
    for _ in range(4):
        if (rp / ".git").exists() or (rp / BIBLES_DIR).exists():
            return rp
        rp = rp.parent
    return arg_path.resolve()

def list_bibles(repo: Path):
    path = repo / BIBLES_DIR
    files = []
    if path.exists():
        for p in sorted(path.glob("N??_Bible_*.md")):
            files.append(p.relative_to(repo).as_posix())
    return files

def extract_num(fname: str) -> int | None:
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Bible_", fname)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

def grep_file(path: Path, needles: list[str]) -> dict[str, int]:
    try:
        txt = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except Exception:
        return {k: 0 for k in needles}
    out = {}
    for n in needles:
        out[n] = len(re.findall(re.escape(n), txt))
    return out

def grep_dir(root: Path, needles: list[str]) -> list[tuple[str, dict[str, int]]]:
    hits = []
    if not root.exists():
        return hits
    for p in root.rglob("*"):
        if p.is_file() and p.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml", ".json"}:
            counts = grep_file(p, needles)
            if sum(counts.values()) > 0:
                hits.append((p.as_posix(), counts))
    return hits

def git_recent_commits(repo: Path, paths: list[Path], n=15) -> list[dict]:
    try:
        base_cmd = ["git", "-C", str(repo), "log", f"-n{n}", "--date=iso", "--pretty=%h%x09%ad%x09%an%x09%s", "--"]
        cmd = base_cmd + [str(p) for p in paths]
        out = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, check=False)
        lines = out.stdout.strip().splitlines()
        rows = []
        for ln in lines:
            if not ln.strip(): 
                continue
            parts = ln.split("\t")
            if len(parts) >= 4:
                rows.append({"sha": parts[0], "date": parts[1], "author": parts[2], "subject": "\t".join(parts[3:])})
        return rows
    except Exception:
        return []

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print(__doc__)
        sys.exit(2)
    repo = find_repo_root(Path(sys.argv[1]))
    write = ("--write" in sys.argv)
    report_md = repo / "omnimeta_audit_report.md"
    report_json = repo / "omnimeta_audit_summary.json"

    # 1) Bible files audit
    bibles = list_bibles(repo)
    nums = [extract_num(f) for f in bibles]
    present = sorted([n for n in nums if n is not None])
    missing = [i for i in range(1,31) if i not in present]
    dupes = [n for n in set(present) if present.count(n) > 1]
    by_num = defaultdict(list)
    for f in bibles:
        n = extract_num(f)
        if n is not None:
            by_num[n].append(f)

    # 2) Title propagation audit
    needles_old = [OLD_TITLES[28], OLD_TITLES[29]]
    needles_new = [CORRECT_TITLES[28], CORRECT_TITLES[29]]

    timeline_counts = grep_file(repo / TIMELINE, needles_old + needles_new)
    spine_counts = grep_file(repo / STORY_SPINE, needles_old + needles_new)
    prose_hits = grep_dir(repo / PROSE_DIR, needles_old)

    # 3) N28/N29 file name check
    n28_files = by_num.get(28, [])
    n29_files = by_num.get(29, [])
    n28_ok = any("ECHOES_END" in f for f in n28_files)
    n29_ok = any("APEX_OF_STASIS" in f for f in n29_files)

    # 4) recent commits
    recent = git_recent_commits(repo, [BIBLES_DIR, TIMELINE, STORY_SPINE, PROSE_DIR])

    summary = {
        "repo": str(repo),
        "bibles_found": len(bibles),
        "bibles_missing_numbers": missing,
        "duplicates": {str(k): v for k, v in {n: by_num[n] for n in dupes}.items()},
        "n28_files": n28_files,
        "n29_files": n29_files,
        "n28_filename_correct": n28_ok,
        "n29_filename_correct": n29_ok,
        "timeline_counts": timeline_counts,
        "story_spine_counts": spine_counts,
        "prose_old_title_hits": prose_hits,
        "recent_commits": recent,
    }

    # Build Markdown report
    def fmt_counts(lbl, d):
        if not d:
            return f"- {lbl}: file not found"
        rows = [f"- **{k}**: {v}" for k, v in d.items()]
        return "\n".join(rows)

    md = [MD_HEADER]
    md.append(f"**Repo root:** `{summary['repo']}`\n")
    md.append("## Bible files\n")
    md.append(f"- Found: **{summary['bibles_found']}** (expect 30)\n")
    if summary['bibles_missing_numbers']:
        md.append(f"- Missing N#: {', '.join(f'N{n:02d}' for n in summary['bibles_missing_numbers'])}\n")
    if summary['duplicates']:
        md.append("- Duplicates:\n")
        for n, files in summary['duplicates'].items():
            md.append(f"  - N{int(n):02d}:")
            for f in files:
                md.append(f"    - `{f}`")
    md.append("\n### N28/N29 filename sanity\n")
    md.append(f"- N28 filename OK (contains `ECHOES_END`): **{summary['n28_filename_correct']}**")
    md.append(f"- N29 filename OK (contains `APEX_OF_STASIS`): **{summary['n29_filename_correct']}**\n")

    md.append("## Timeline & Story-Spine title propagation\n")
    md.append("### Timeline\n")
    md.append(fmt_counts("Timeline", summary["timeline_counts"]) + "\n")
    md.append("### Story Spine\n")
    md.append(fmt_counts("Story Spine", summary["story_spine_counts"]) + "\n")

    md.append("## Prose Engines — old title references\n")
    if not summary["prose_old_title_hits"]:
        md.append("- No occurrences of old titles found in prose engines.\n")
    else:
        md.append("- Files referencing old titles:\n")
        for f, cnts in summary["prose_old_title_hits"]:
            md.append(f"  - `{f}` — " + ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k, v in cnts.items() if v))

    if summary["recent_commits"]:
        md.append("\n## Recent commits touching relevant areas\n")
        md.append("| SHA | Date | Author | Subject |\n|---|---|---|---|")
        for r in summary["recent_commits"]:
            md.append(f"| `{r['sha']}` | {r['date']} | {r['author']} | {r['subject']} |")

    md_text = "\n".join(md)

    if write:
        (repo / "omnimeta_audit_report.md").write_text(md_text, encoding="utf-8")
        (repo / "omnimeta_audit_summary.json").write_text(json.dumps(summary, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
        print(f"Wrote: {report_md}")
        print(f"Wrote: {report_json}")
    else:

# Write the repo audit script to the sandbox so the user can download/run it locally.
from pathlib import Path

audit_path = Path("/mnt/data/omnimeta_repo_audit.py")

audit_code = r'''#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
OmniMeta repo audit — checks title normalization & file layout.

Usage:
  python3 omnimeta_repo_audit.py /path/to/your/repo  [--write]

If --write is passed, the report files will be written into the repo root as:
  - omnimeta_audit_report.md
  - omnimeta_audit_summary.json
Otherwise, results are printed to stdout.

What it checks:
  1) 30 Bible files present and uniquely numbered (N01..N30)
  2) N28/N29 titles propagated: "Echoes End" / "Apex of Stasis"
     and the old titles ("All Constructs Fall" / "Knotted Resolution") are absent
  3) Timeline & Story-Spine contain the corrected titles
  4) Prose engines contain no references to old titles
  5) Optional: the last 15 commits that touched relevant files/directories (if git is available)
"""

import sys, os, re, json, subprocess, textwrap
from pathlib import Path
from collections import defaultdict

CORRECT_TITLES = {
    28: "Echoes End",
    29: "Apex of Stasis",
}
OLD_TITLES = {
    28: "All Constructs Fall",
    29: "Knotted Resolution",
}

# Repo structure of interest
BIBLES_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles")
TIMELINE = Path("03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md")
STORY_SPINE = Path("03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md")
PROSE_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES")

def list_bibles(repo: Path):
    path = repo / BIBLES_DIR
    files = []
    if path.exists():
        for p in sorted(path.glob("N??_Bible_*.md")):
            files.append(p.relative_to(repo).as_posix())
    return files

def extract_num(fname: str):
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Bible_", fname)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

def grep_file(path: Path, needles):
    try:
        txt = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except Exception:
        return {k: 0 for k in needles}
    out = {}
    for n in needles:
        out[n] = len(re.findall(re.escape(n), txt))
    return out

def grep_dir(root: Path, needles):
    hits = []
    if not root.exists():
        return hits
    for p in root.rglob("*"):
        if p.is_file() and p.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml", ".json"}:
            counts = grep_file(p, needles)
            if sum(counts.values()) > 0:
                hits.append((p.as_posix(), counts))
    return hits

def git_recent_commits(repo: Path, paths, n=15):
    try:
        base_cmd = ["git", "-C", str(repo), "log", f"-n{n}", "--date=iso", "--pretty=%h%x09%ad%x09%an%x09%s", "--"]
        cmd = base_cmd + [str(p) for p in paths]
        out = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, check=False)
        lines = out.stdout.strip().splitlines()
        rows = []
        for ln in lines:
            if not ln.strip(): 
                continue
            parts = ln.split("\t")
            if len(parts) >= 4:
                rows.append({"sha": parts[0], "date": parts[1], "author": parts[2], "subject": "\t".join(parts[3:])})
        return rows
    except Exception:
        return []

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print(__doc__)
        sys.exit(2)
    repo = Path(sys.argv[1]).resolve()
    write = ("--write" in sys.argv)

    # 1) Bible files audit
    bibles = list_bibles(repo)
    nums = [extract_num(f) for f in bibles]
    present = sorted([n for n in nums if n is not None])
    missing = [i for i in range(1,31) if i not in present]
    dupes = [n for n in set(present) if present.count(n) > 1]
    by_num = defaultdict(list)
    for f in bibles:
        n = extract_num(f)
        if n is not None:
            by_num[n].append(f)

    # 2) Title propagation audit
    needles_old = [OLD_TITLES[28], OLD_TITLES[29]]
    needles_new = [CORRECT_TITLES[28], CORRECT_TITLES[29]]

    timeline_counts = grep_file(repo / TIMELINE, needles_old + needles_new)
    spine_counts = grep_file(repo / STORY_SPINE, needles_old + needles_new)
    prose_hits = grep_dir(repo / PROSE_DIR, needles_old)

    # 3) N28/N29 file name check
    n28_files = by_num.get(28, [])
    n29_files = by_num.get(29, [])
    n28_ok = any("ECHOES_END" in f for f in n28_files)
    n29_ok = any("APEX_OF_STASIS" in f for f in n29_files)

    # 4) recent commits
    recent = git_recent_commits(repo, [BIBLES_DIR, TIMELINE, STORY_SPINE, PROSE_DIR])

    summary = {
        "repo": str(repo),
        "bibles_found": len(bibles),
        "bibles_missing_numbers": missing,
        "duplicates": {str(k): v for k, v in {n: by_num[n] for n in dupes}.items()},
        "n28_files": n28_files,
        "n29_files": n29_files,
        "n28_filename_correct": n28_ok,
        "n29_filename_correct": n29_ok,
        "timeline_counts": timeline_counts,
        "story_spine_counts": spine_counts,
        "prose_old_title_hits": prose_hits,
        "recent_commits": recent,
    }

    # Build Markdown report
    md = []
    md.append("# OmniMeta Repository Audit Report\n")
    md.append(f"**Repo root:** `{summary['repo']}`\n")
    md.append("## Bible files\n")
    md.append(f"- Found: **{summary['bibles_found']}** (expect 30)\n")
    if summary['bibles_missing_numbers']:
        md.append(f"- Missing N#: {', '.join(f'N{n:02d}' for n in summary['bibles_missing_numbers'])}\n")
    if summary['duplicates']:
        md.append("- Duplicates:\n")
        for n, files in summary['duplicates'].items():
            md.append(f"  - N{int(n):02d}:")
            for f in files:
                md.append(f"    - `{f}`")

    md.append("\n### N28/N29 filename sanity\n")
    md.append(f"- N28 filename OK (contains `ECHOES_END`): **{summary['n28_filename_correct']}**\n")
    md.append(f"- N29 filename OK (contains `APEX_OF_STASIS`): **{summary['n29_filename_correct']}**\n")

    def fmt_counts(d):
        if not d:
            return "(file missing)"
        return ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k, v in d.items())

    md.append("## Timeline & Story-Spine title propagation\n")
    md.append(f"- Timeline: {fmt_counts(summary['timeline_counts'])}\n")
    md.append(f"- Story Spine: {fmt_counts(summary['story_spine_counts'])}\n")

    md.append("## Prose Engines — any old title references\n")
    if not summary["prose_old_title_hits"]:
        md.append("- None found.\n")
    else:
        for f, cnts in summary["prose_old_title_hits"]:
            md.append(f"- `{f}` — " + ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k, v in cnts.items() if v))

    if summary["recent_commits"]:
        md.append("\n## Recent commits touching relevant areas\n")
        md.append("| SHA | Date | Author | Subject |\n|---|---|---|---|")
        for r in summary["recent_commits"]:
            md.append(f"| `{r['sha']}` | {r['date']} | {r['author']} | {r['subject']} |")

    md_text = "\n".join(md)

    if write:
        (repo / "omnimeta_audit_report.md").write_text(md_text, encoding="utf-8")
        (repo / "omnimeta_audit_summary.json").write_text(json.dumps(summary, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
        print("Wrote omnimeta_audit_report.md and omnimeta_audit_summary.json")
    else:
        print(md_text)
        print("\nJSON summary:\n" + json.dumps(summary, indent=2))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
'''

audit_path.write_text(audit_code, encoding="utf-8")
audit_path.chmod(0o755)

print(f"Saved audit script to: {audit_path}")

## TL;DR
- Repo is **v2.0** with initial structure and docs; **no `04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles/` directory** is present, and I don’t see your batch of N16–N30 bibles in-tree. The writer deliverables currently show only the **`PROSE_ENGINES/`** folder with an **N1 example** per the README. citeturn0view0
- Commit history visible right now is from **Oct 31, 2025**, including “Complete… v2.0” and “Remove GitHub workflow (permission issue)”. Nothing newer is showing on `main`. If you pushed to a different branch or a fork, it’s not visible here. citeturn5view0
- Root has **`BIBLE_PLACEHOLDER_TEMPLATE.md`** and **`QUICKSTART_BIBLE_GENERATION.md`**, which implies the repo is primed for bibles but they’re not checked in yet. citeturn0view0
- Timelines directory exists with **`01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md`** etc., so your title normalization (N28/N29) should land there—but I can’t verify the text changes from the web UI because GitHub code search is gated and the file viewer is being temperamental without auth. The structure is correct though. citeturn0view0

If you “made those changes in your own way,” they’re either not on `main`, not pushed, or pushed to a private fork. From the public `main`, the bibles and N28/N29 renames aren’t present.

## What’s missing vs your plan

  - `03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md`
  - any `PROSE_ENGINES/**` references  
  also can’t be verified from the web UI, only locally.

## Quick path to align repo with the plan
You’ve got two options. Pick your flavor:

### Option A — push the updated files now (fastest)
1) Download my apply script and run it against your repo with your ZIP of corrected bibles:
   - Script: **[omnimeta_apply.sh](sandbox:/mnt/data/omnimeta_apply.sh)**
   - Your ZIP: **[corrected_omnimeta_files.zip](sandbox:/mnt/data/corrected_omnimeta_files.zip)**
2) Run:
```bash
export REPO_URL=git@github.com:ElinVoss/omnimeta-saga-universe.git
export ZIP_PATH=/absolute/path/to/corrected_omnimeta_files.zip
export OPEN_PR=true
bash omnimeta_apply.sh
```
The script:
- creates `04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles/` if missing,
- layers in your N16–N30 files without deleting anything (until all 30 exist),
- normalizes N28→**Echoes End** and N29→**Apex of Stasis** across timelines/spine/prose,
- commits, pushes, and opens a PR.

### Option B — prove the current state with a local audit (zero guesswork)
I dropped a small audit tool you can run locally on any branch/clone:

- **[Download omnimeta_repo_audit.py](sandbox:/mnt/data/omnimeta_repo_audit.py)**

Usage:
```bash
python3 omnimeta_repo_audit.py /path/to/clone --write
```
It outputs:
- missing N## bibles,
- whether N28/N29 filenames are correctly renamed,
- counts of old vs new titles in the timeline and story-spine,
- any leftover old titles in `PROSE_ENGINES/`,
- last 15 commits touching those paths.

## Recommended next moves (practical, no fluff)
1) If your changes live locally: run the audit script, then push a branch and open a PR.  
2) If they’re on another branch already: link me the branch; I’ll do a line-by-line diff review and prep a cleanup PR description.  
3) If you intentionally *don’t* want to store all 30 bibles in Git (size/privacy): commit only a **manifest** + **generation inputs**, keep bibles in a release artifact or GH Pages, and wire a GitHub Action to regenerate on `workflow_dispatch`. That avoids repo bloat and still feeds your agents reliably.

Bottom line: the public `main` doesn’t show the bibles or N28/N29 work yet. Either push your branch, or run the apply script and we’ll codify it as a clean PR.

# Inspect the uploaded repo ZIP, audit for Bible files and N28/N29 title propagation,
# and write a Markdown report for you to download.
import os, zipfile, re, json, textwrap, shutil
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

ZIP_PATH = Path("/mnt/data/omnimeta-saga-universe-main.zip")
workdir = Path("/mnt/data/_audit_workspace")
if workdir.exists():
    shutil.rmtree(workdir)
workdir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

assert ZIP_PATH.exists(), f"ZIP not found at {ZIP_PATH}"

# Unzip
with zipfile.ZipFile(ZIP_PATH) as z:
    z.extractall(workdir)

# Find repo root (top-level dir that contains expected folders)
candidates = [p for p in workdir.iterdir() if p.is_dir()]
repo_root = None
for c in candidates:
    if (c / "04_Writer_Deliverables").exists() or (c / "03_Structural_Timelines").exists():
        repo_root = c
        break
repo_root = repo_root or workdir

# Paths of interest
BIBLES_DIR = repo_root / "04_Writer_Deliverables" / "02_Bibles"
TIMELINE = repo_root / "03_Structural_Timelines" / "01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md"
STORY_SPINE = repo_root / "03_Structural_Timelines" / "09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md"
PROSE_DIR = repo_root / "04_Writer_Deliverables" / "PROSE_ENGINES"

CORRECT_TITLES = {28: "Echoes End", 29: "Apex of Stasis"}
OLD_TITLES = {28: "All Constructs Fall", 29: "Knotted Resolution"}

def list_bibles():
    files = []
    if BIBLES_DIR.exists():
        for p in sorted(BIBLES_DIR.glob("N??_Bible_*.md")):
            files.append(p)
    return files

def extract_num(path: Path):
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Bible_", path.name)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

def read_text(p: Path):
    try:
        return p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except Exception:
        return ""

def count_occurrences(text: str, needles):
    return {needle: len(re.findall(re.escape(needle), text)) for needle in needles}

# Gather Bible stats
bible_paths = list_bibles()
nums_present = sorted([n for n in (extract_num(p) for p in bible_paths) if n is not None])
missing_nums = [i for i in range(1,31) if i not in nums_present]
dupes = sorted({n for n in nums_present if nums_present.count(n) > 1})

# N28/N29 filename sanity
n28_files = [p for p in bible_paths if extract_num(p) == 28]
n29_files = [p for p in bible_paths if extract_num(p) == 29]
n28_ok = any("ECHOES_END" in p.name for p in n28_files)
n29_ok = any("APEX_OF_STASIS" in p.name for p in n29_files)

# Timeline & Spine text checks
timeline_text = read_text(TIMELINE)
spine_text = read_text(STORY_SPINE)
timeline_counts = count_occurrences(timeline_text, [OLD_TITLES[28], OLD_TITLES[29], CORRECT_TITLES[28], CORRECT_TITLES[29]]) if timeline_text else {}
spine_counts = count_occurrences(spine_text, [OLD_TITLES[28], OLD_TITLES[29], CORRECT_TITLES[28], CORRECT_TITLES[29]]) if spine_text else {}

# Prose engines scan for old titles
prose_hits = []
if PROSE_DIR.exists():
    for p in PROSE_DIR.rglob("*"):
        if p.is_file() and p.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml", ".json"}:
            t = read_text(p)
            counts = count_occurrences(t, [OLD_TITLES[28], OLD_TITLES[29]])
            if sum(counts.values()) > 0:
                prose_hits.append((str(p.relative_to(repo_root)), counts))

# Build Markdown report
report_lines = []
report_lines.append("# OmniMeta Repository Audit Report")
report_lines.append(f"_Generated: {datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}Z_")
report_lines.append(f"**Repo root detected:** `{repo_root.name}`\n")

report_lines.append("## Bible files")
report_lines.append(f"- Path present: **{BIBLES_DIR.exists()}**  (`{BIBLES_DIR.relative_to(repo_root) if BIBLES_DIR.exists() else 'missing'}`)")
report_lines.append(f"- Bible files found: **{len(bible_paths)}** (expect 30)")
if bible_paths:
    sample = "\n".join(f"  - {p.name}" for p in bible_paths[:10])
    report_lines.append("### First few files\n" + sample)
if missing_nums:
    report_lines.append(f"- Missing numbers: {', '.join(f'N{n:02d}' for n in missing_nums)}")
if dupes:
    report_lines.append(f"- Duplicate numbers: {', '.join(f'N{n:02d}' for n in dupes)}")

report_lines.append("\n### Late BREAK filenames")
report_lines.append(f"- N28 filename OK (contains `ECHOES_END`): **{n28_ok}**")
report_lines.append(f"- N29 filename OK (contains `APEX_OF_STASIS`): **{n29_ok}**")
if n28_files:
    report_lines.append("  - N28 files:\n" + "\n".join(f"    - {p.name}" for p in n28_files))
if n29_files:
    report_lines.append("  - N29 files:\n" + "\n".join(f"    - {p.name}" for p in n29_files))

report_lines.append("\n## Timeline & Story-Spine Title Propagation")
report_lines.append(f"- Timeline file present: **{TIMELINE.exists()}**")
if TIMELINE.exists():
    report_lines.append("  - Counts: " + ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k,v in timeline_counts.items()))
report_lines.append(f"- Story spine file present: **{STORY_SPINE.exists()}**")
if STORY_SPINE.exists():
    report_lines.append("  - Counts: " + ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k,v in spine_counts.items()))

report_lines.append("\n## Prose Engines — old title references")
if not PROSE_DIR.exists():
    report_lines.append("- `04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES` not found.")
elif not prose_hits:
    report_lines.append("- No references to old titles found.")
else:
    report_lines.append("- Files referencing old titles:")
    for relpath, counts in prose_hits:
        report_lines.append(f"  - `{relpath}` — " + ", ".join(f"{k}: {v}" for k,v in counts.items() if v))

# Save report
report_path = Path("/mnt/data/omnimeta_audit_report.md")
report_md = "\n".join(report_lines)
report_path.write_text(report_md, encoding="utf-8")

# Also print a concise JSON summary for quick view in the notebook
summary = {
    "repo_root": repo_root.name,
    "bibles_dir_exists": BIBLES_DIR.exists(),
    "bibles_found": len(bible_paths),
    "missing_numbers": missing_nums,
    "n28_filename_ok": n28_ok,
    "n29_filename_ok": n29_ok,
    "timeline_present": TIMELINE.exists(),
    "timeline_counts": timeline_counts,
    "story_spine_present": STORY_SPINE.exists(),
    "story_spine_counts": spine_counts,
    "prose_hits_count": len(prose_hits),
}
print(json.dumps(summary, indent=2))
print("\nSaved report to:", str(report_path))

# Re-audit counting both .md and .txt Bible files, then regenerate the report.
import re, json
from pathlib import Path

repo_root = Path("/mnt/data/_audit_workspace/omnimeta-saga-universe-main")
bibles_dir = repo_root / "04_Writer_Deliverables" / "02_Bibles"

def extract_num(name: str):
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Bible_", name)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

files = sorted([p for p in bibles_dir.glob("N??_Bible_*.*") if p.suffix.lower() in (".md", ".txt")])
nums = [extract_num(p.name) for p in files]
present = sorted(n for n in nums if n is not None)
missing = [i for i in range(1,31) if i not in present]
by_num = {}
for p in files:
    n = extract_num(p.name)
    by_num.setdefault(n, []).append(p.name)

# Check late-break filenames regardless of extension
n28_names = by_num.get(28, [])
n29_names = by_num.get(29, [])
n28_ok = any("ECHOES_END" in n for n in n28_names)
n29_ok = any("APEX_OF_STASIS" in n for n in n29_names)

summary = {
    "total_bibles": len(files),
    "present_numbers": present,
    "missing_numbers": missing,
    "n01_n15_extensions": {name: Path(name).suffix for name in [n for n in sum((by_num.get(i, []) for i in range(1,16)), [])]},
    "n16_n30_extensions": {name: Path(name).suffix for name in [n for n in sum((by_num.get(i, []) for i in range(16,31)), [])]},
    "n28_names": n28_names,
    "n29_names": n29_names,
    "n28_filename_ok": n28_ok,
    "n29_filename_ok": n29_ok,
}
print(json.dumps(summary, indent=2))

# Save a v2 audit script that treats N01–N15 as .txt and N16–N30 as .md (or any mix).
from pathlib import Path
audit_v2_path = Path("/mnt/data/omnimeta_repo_audit_v2.py")
code = r'''#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, re, json, subprocess
from pathlib import Path
from collections import defaultdict

BIBLES_SUBDIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles")
TIMELINE = Path("03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md")
STORY_SPINE = Path("03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md")
PROSE_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/PROSE_ENGINES")

CORRECT = {28: "Echoes End", 29: "Apex of Stasis"}
OLD = {28: "All Constructs Fall", 29: "Knotted Resolution"}

def extract_num(name: str):
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Bible_", name)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

def read_text(p: Path):
    try: return p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except: return ""

def grep_counts(p: Path, terms):
    if not p.exists(): return {}
    t = read_text(p)
    return {term: (t.count(term)) for term in terms}

def scan_dir(root: Path, terms):
    hits = []
    if not root.exists(): return hits
    for p in root.rglob("*"):
        if p.is_file() and p.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml", ".json"}:
            t = read_text(p)
            c = {term: t.count(term) for term in terms}
            if sum(c.values()): hits.append((p.as_posix(), c))
    return hits

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print("Usage: python3 omnimeta_repo_audit_v2.py /path/to/clone [--write]")
        sys.exit(2)
    repo = Path(sys.argv[1]).resolve()
    write = ("--write" in sys.argv)
    bibles_dir = repo / BIBLES_SUBDIR

    bibles = sorted(
        [p for p in bibles_dir.glob("N??_Bible_*.*") if p.suffix.lower() in (".md",".txt")],
        key=lambda p: p.name
    )
    present = [extract_num(p.name) for p in bibles if extract_num(p.name) is not None]
    missing = [i for i in range(1,31) if i not in present]

    by_num = defaultdict(list)
    for p in bibles:
        n = extract_num(p.name)
        if n is not None: by_num[n].append(p.name)

    n28_ok = any("ECHOES_END" in n for n in by_num.get(28, []))
    n29_ok = any("APEX_OF_STASIS" in n for n in by_num.get(29, []))

    timeline_counts = grep_counts(repo / TIMELINE, [OLD[28], OLD[29], CORRECT[28], CORRECT[29]])
    spine_counts = grep_counts(repo / STORY_SPINE, [OLD[28], OLD[29], CORRECT[28], CORRECT[29]])
    prose_hits = scan_dir(repo / PROSE_DIR, [OLD[28], OLD[29]])

    summary = {
        "bibles_dir": str(BIBLES_SUBDIR),
        "bibles_found": len(bibles),
        "missing_numbers": missing,
        "by_num": dict(by_num),
        "n28_filename_ok": n28_ok,
        "n29_filename_ok": n29_ok,
        "timeline_counts": timeline_counts,
        "story_spine_counts": spine_counts,
        "prose_hits": prose_hits,
    }

    md = []
    md.append("# OmniMeta Repo Audit v2\n")
    md.append(f"- Bibles dir: `{BIBLES_SUBDIR}`")
    md.append(f"- Found Bible files: **{len(bibles)}**")
    if missing: md.append(f"- Missing N#: {', '.join(f'N{n:02d}' for n in missing)}")
    md.append("\n### N28/N29 filenames\n")
    md.append(f"- N28 OK (`ECHOES_END` in name): **{n28_ok}**")
    md.append(f"- N29 OK (`APEX_OF_STASIS` in name): **{n29_ok}**\n")
    md.append("### Timeline / Story-Spine counts")
    md.append(f"- Timeline: {summary['timeline_counts']}")
    md.append(f"- Story Spine: {summary['story_spine_counts']}\n")
    md.append("### Prose old-title hits")
    if not prose_hits: md.append("- None")
    else:
        for f, cnts in prose_hits:
            md.append(f"- `{f}` — {cnts}")
    md_text = "\n".join(md)

    if write:
        (repo / "omnimeta_audit_report_v2.md").write_text(md_text, encoding="utf-8")
        print("Wrote omnimeta_audit_report_v2.md")
    else:
        print(md_text)
        print("\nJSON summary:\n" + json.dumps(summary, indent=2))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
'''
audit_v2_path.write_text(code, encoding="utf-8")
audit_v2_path.chmod(0o755)
print(f"Saved: {audit_v2_path}")

it will:

## 2) future-proof the apply flow
if you want the “agent mode” apply script to respect both extensions, tweak the copy/rename blocks to handle `*.md` **and** `*.txt`. here’s the drop-in change:

```bash
# copy both .md and .txt bibles if present
shopt -s nullglob
for ext in md txt; do
  rsync -a "$srcroot"/N??_Bible_*."$ext" "$BIBLES_DIR"/ 2>/dev/null || true
done

# rename N28/N29 regardless of extension
for ext in md txt; do
  [[ -f "$BIBLES_DIR/N28_Bible_ALL_CONSTRUCTS_FALL.$ext" ]] && \
    git mv -f "$BIBLES_DIR/N28_Bible_ALL_CONSTRUCTS_FALL.$ext" "$BIBLES_DIR/N28_Bible_ECHOES_END.$ext" || \
    mv -f "$BIBLES_DIR/N28_Bible_ALL_CONSTRUCTS_FALL.$ext" "$BIBLES_DIR/N28_Bible_ECHOES_END.$ext" 2>/dev/null || true

  [[ -f "$BIBLES_DIR/N29_Bible_KNOTTED_RESOLUTION.$ext" ]] && \
    git mv -f "$BIBLES_DIR/N29_Bible_KNOTTED_RESOLUTION.$ext" "$BIBLES_DIR/N29_Bible_APEX_OF_STASIS.$ext" || \
    mv -f "$BIBLES_DIR/N29_Bible_KNOTTED_RESOLUTION.$ext" "$BIBLES_DIR/N29_Bible_APEX_OF_STASIS.$ext" 2>/dev/null || true
done
```

## do you want to standardize?
mixed extensions are fine operationally, but teams forget. if you want everything `.md`, here’s a safe, reversible renamer:

```bash
cd 04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles
# preview
ls N??_Bible_*.txt | sed 's/.txt$/.md/'

# do it (git tracks renames)
for f in N??_Bible_*.txt; do
  [[ -f "$f" ]] && git mv "$f" "${f%.txt}.md"
done
git commit -m "Normalize Bible files to .md (N01–N15)"
```

## 1) add a consistency check script
**.github/scripts/verify_consistency.sh**
```bash
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

ROOT="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel 2>/dev/null || pwd)"
cd "$ROOT"

BIBLES_DIR="04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles"
TIMELINE="03_Structural_Timelines/01_Progression_Timeline_Master.md"
STORY_SPINE="03_Structural_Timelines/09_Story_Spine_Mapping_Innocent.md"

err(){ echo "❌ $*" >&2; exit 1; }

[[ -d "$BIBLES_DIR" ]] || err "Missing $BIBLES_DIR"

shopt -s nullglob
mapfile -t BIBLES < <(ls "$BIBLES_DIR"/N??_Bible_*.* 2>/dev/null | grep -E '\.(md|txt)$' || true)
((${#BIBLES[@]})) || err "No Bible files found"

declare -A seen
for path in "${BIBLES[@]}"; do
  f="$(basename "$path")"
  [[ "$f" =~ ^N[0-9]{2}_Bible_.*\.(md|txt)$ ]] || err "Bad filename: $f"
  n="${f:1:2}"                         # from N??_
  [[ -z "${seen[$n]:-}" ]] || err "Duplicate for N$n: ${seen[$n]} and $f"
  seen[$n]="$f"
done

# ensure exactly one file for each N01..N30 (either .md or .txt)
for n in $(seq -w 01 30); do
  [[ -n "${seen[$n]:-}" ]] || err "Missing Bible file for N$n"
done

# late-BREAK filenames must be the corrected canon
[[ "${seen[28],,}" =~ n28_bible_echoes_end\.(md|txt)$ ]] || err "N28 must be ECHOES_END (found: ${seen[28]:-missing})"
[[ "${seen[29],,}" =~ n29_bible_apex_of_stasis\.(md|txt)$ ]] || err "N29 must be APEX_OF_STASIS (found: ${seen[29]:-missing})"

# no old titles anywhere
if git grep -nE 'All Constructs Fall|Knotted Resolution' -- . >/dev/null; then
  git grep -nE 'All Constructs Fall|Knotted Resolution' -- .
  err "Old titles still present"
fi

# new titles must appear in timeline & spine
grep -q 'Echoes End' "$TIMELINE"       || err "Echoes End missing from timeline"
grep -q 'Apex of Stasis' "$TIMELINE"   || err "Apex of Stasis missing from timeline"
grep -q 'Echoes End' "$STORY_SPINE"    || err "Echoes End missing from story spine"
grep -q 'Apex of Stasis' "$STORY_SPINE"|| err "Apex of Stasis missing from story spine"

echo "✅ Consistency check passed."
```

Nice. You’ve basically turned the repo into a self-defending library. Since Actions were blocked when you tried to add the workflow, here are clean, no-drama ways to make those checks run automatically anyway—and a ready-to-drop workflow for when permissions are fixed.

## zero-permissions automation (runs on PRs without a workflow file)
Use **pre-commit.ci**. It piggybacks on your `.pre-commit-config.yaml` and runs on every PR without needing `.github/workflows/*`.

1) Add this to the repo root:

```yaml
# .pre-commit-config.yaml
repos:
  - repo: local
    hooks:
      - id: omnimeta-consistency
        name: omnimeta-consistency
        entry: bash .github/scripts/verify_consistency.sh
        language: system
        pass_filenames: false
```

2) Go to pre-commit.ci, enable the repo. That’s it. Every PR will run your shell guard and fail fast if anything drifts.

## local + dev-env ergonomics
Give folks a one-command check:

```makefile
# Makefile
verify:
	@bash .github/scripts/verify_consistency.sh
```

and/or:

```json
// package.json (if you’ve got Node around)
{
  "scripts": {
    "verify": "bash .github/scripts/verify_consistency.sh"
  }
}
```

## when Actions permissions get sorted
Drop this in:

```yaml
# .github/workflows/consistency.yml
name: omnimeta-consistency
on:
  pull_request:
  push:
    branches: [main]
permissions:
  contents: read
jobs:
  verify:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - run: bash .github/scripts/verify_consistency.sh
```

If the blocker was repo settings, the owner can flip:
- Settings → Actions → General → “Allow GitHub Actions to run”, and set **Workflow permissions** to at least **Read repository contents**. You don’t need write perms for this job.

## branch protection (makes it bite)
In Settings → Branches → Branch protection rules for `main`:
- Require status checks to pass before merging
- Add the check name (from pre-commit.ci or the workflow above)
- Block force pushes

---

Bottom line: your shell guard + PR template already kill the human-error cases. Add **pre-commit.ci** today for automatic PR enforcement, then wire the GitHub Action once permissions allow. From here, consistency regressions don’t sneak in—they faceplant loudly.

i think im ready for the perplexity space to automate the bible gen prompts and instructions for each gpt. what you think? is the narrative great story there? is it going to be engaging? is there enough actionable material to be worth reading?

[ASSISTANT]
Short answer: yes—you’re ready to automate. The repo’s structure + guardrails are solid. You’ve got a clean canon, consistent late-BREAK titles, and a scriptable surface area. That’s exactly what a “perplexity space” (or any agent loop) wants.

Now the spicy, useful part:

## Is the story engaging?
From the scaffolding and the node titles, you’ve got a classic escalating pressure curve from N01→N30 with a late-BREAK payoff (“Echoes End” → “Apex of Stasis”). That’s fertile ground. Where stories die is in mushy mid-nodes and vibe-only bibles. If your bibles actually include concrete **conflict**, **stakes**, and **irreversible choices** per node, you’re golden. If they lean abstract (“themes,” “tone,” “world feels”) without **sceneable** beats, expect fluffy output.

### 7 quick engagement checks (brutal but fair)
For any node (pick N17, N23, N28), you should be able to point to:
1) A **curiosity gap** in the first three sentences.  
2) A **goal–obstacle–decision** triangle, not just “exploration happens.”  
3) A **cost** for success and a **consequence** for failure—named, not implied.  
4) A **reversal** or reveal that changes the plan.  
5) A **specific image** the reader can see (not vibes; a concrete beat).  
6) A **character shift** (belief or relationship moves by one click).  
7) A **promise for the next node** (clear handoff).

If any node fails ≥2 of these, it’ll feel meh when automated. Fix the bible, not the model.

## Is there enough actionable material?
Actionable = the model can **do** something deterministic with it. Each bible should include:
- **Logline** (one-sentence mandate)  
- **Beat list** (3–7 bullets with verbs and outcomes)  
- **Must-include details** (canon facts, names, objects, phrases)  
- **Banned moves** (no-go tropes, tone bans, forbidden reveals)  
- **Continuity hooks** (what it must inherit + what it must set up)  
- **Acceptance criteria** (how we decide the output is “done”)  

If those sections exist per node, you’ve got fuel. If not, add them; the rest is just plumbing.

---

## How to wire “Perplexity Space” without chaos
Make it a 3-stage agent chain and keep it boringly deterministic.

### Stage A — Generator (per node)
**System**: “You are the *Bible Generator* for Node NXX. Follow schema. Never invent outside canon. Quote source lines when you infer.”  
**User**: YAML frontmatter + constraints + beat list.  
**Output**: JSON or Markdown with **fixed keys** only.

**Minimal schema (YAML frontmatter + sections):**
```yaml
node: N23
title: EACH_FACTION_STANDS
inherits:
  - N22.outcome: "Trust collapse after test"
must_include:
  - Object: "Signal Key Sigma"
  - Location: "Ravel Bridge"
banned:
  - Deus ex machina
  - Amnesia twist
acceptance:
  - Includes one irreversible choice
  - Sets a concrete timer/pressure element
---
# Beats
- Goal: Hold the bridge long enough to broadcast.
- Obstacle: Jammer oscillates; friendly fire risk.
- Decision: Protagonist destroys allied buffer to boost signal.
# Scene Seeds
- Image: frozen vapor off ruptured coolant lines
- Line: “It’ll hurt less if you don’t watch.”
# Continuity Hooks
- Next requires: signal partial, retaliation imminent.
```

### Stage B — Continuity Cop
- Validates against **canon dict** (world rules, glossary, character sheets).  
- Fails the output if it contradicts; proposes deltas instead of “fixing” on its own.  
- Emits a **diff** report (“this line violates X; replace with Y”).

### Stage C — Stylistic Surgeon
- Tightens language, preserves facts, checks tone bans.  
- Enforces length, section ordering, and acceptance criteria.

Keep these three roles separate so one bad step doesn’t smear over a contradiction.

---

## Guardrails specific to this project
- **Name Drift Kill-Switch**: a glossary that must be referenced; forbid unseen variants.  
- **Timeline Locks**: NXX cannot resolve a thread introduced at NYY unless a flag is set.  
- **Title Tests**: N28/N29 wording tests (already done script-side) run after generation too.  
- **Refusal Policy**: if a section lacks enough input (e.g., no Must-include), the Generator must **refuse** with a human-readable TODO. Don’t let it hallucinate to fill gaps.

---

## Ready-to-run prompt skeletons
Use these as the base “system prompts” for each actor.

**Bible Generator — System**
```
You are the OmniMeta Bible Generator for node {N}. You must:
- Follow the provided YAML schema and output exactly the same structure.
- Use only canon facts supplied (timeline, spine, glossary).
- If required info is missing, STOP and return a TODO list instead of guessing.
- Cite the exact canon line when you enforce a constraint (e.g., [canon: Timeline §3]).
- Never introduce new proper nouns unless allowed in `allowed_new_terms`.
```

**Continuity Cop — System**
```
You validate a Bible against canon. Tasks:
- Compare all facts with the provided canon bundle.
- Flag contradictions with: {location, offending_text, canon_source, fix_suggestion}.
- If no contradictions, emit "OK" plus a signed checksum (md5 of content).
No rewriting beyond minimal fix suggestions.
```

**Stylistic Surgeon — System**
```
You improve clarity without changing facts:
- Keep sections, keys, and lengths.
- Enforce "no banned moves".
- Replace abstractions with concrete images where Beats require it.
Return the edited content and a bullet list of changes.
```

- **Engagement:** Likely yes, *if* each node bible passes the 7 checks. If some nodes are still theme-forward and beat-light, they’ll read pretty but won’t move.  
- **Actionability:** If your bibles have loglines, beats, must-include, banned moves, and acceptance criteria: **absolutely**. If they don’t: spend one hour per node adding those—ROI is enormous.

[ASSISTANT]
# Scan the uploaded repo snapshot for Bible generation prompts/instructions and summarize key files.
from pathlib import Path
import re, json, textwrap

repo = Path("/mnt/data/_audit_workspace/omnimeta-saga-universe-main")
assert repo.exists(), "Repo snapshot not found. Re-upload if needed."

# Find likely prompt/instruction files
candidates = []
for p in repo.rglob("*"):
    if p.is_file():
        name = p.name.lower()
        if any(k in name for k in [
            "prompt", "generation", "quickstart", "template", "bible_placeholder", "instructions"
        ]):
            # limit to markdown/txt/yaml/json for readability
            if p.suffix.lower() in (".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml", ".json", ""):
                candidates.append(p)

# Prioritize some known ones
priority = []
for wanted in [
    "QUICKSTART_BIBLE_GENERATION.md",
    "BIBLE_PLACEHOLDER_TEMPLATE.md",
    "SourceMap.md",
    "README.md"
]:
    p = repo / wanted
    if p.exists():
        priority.append(p)

# Deduplicate and keep top ~12
seen = set()
ordered = []
for p in priority + candidates:
    if p in seen: 
        continue
    seen.add(p)
    ordered.append(p)
    if len(ordered) >= 12:
        break

def head(p: Path, n=100):
    try:
        txt = p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except Exception:
        return ""
    # collapse multiple blank lines
    lines = txt.strip().splitlines()
    return "\n".join(lines[:n])

summaries = []
for p in ordered:
    content = head(p, 80)
    # crude extraction: find headings and bullets
    headings = [ln.strip("# ").strip() for ln in content.splitlines() if ln.startswith("#")]
    bullets = [ln.strip() for ln in content.splitlines() if ln.strip().startswith(("-", "*"))]
    snippets = "\n".join(content.splitlines()[:20])
    summaries.append({
        "path": str(p.relative_to(repo)),
        "headings": headings[:8],
        "first_lines": snippets
    })

print(json.dumps({
    "found_files": [str(p.relative_to(repo)) for p in ordered],
    "summaries": summaries
}, indent=2))

[ASSISTANT]
Yep. I read the prompt kit in your repo snapshot:

- `QUICKSTART_BIBLE_GENERATION.md`
- `BIBLE_PLACEHOLDER_TEMPLATE.md`
- And the node-specific prompt files like  
  `N01_Prompt_Grip_That_Holds.txt` … through `N09_Prompt_Creations_Test.txt`

### Verdict in one breath
They’re solid and absolutely automatable: each prompt has clear sections—**YOUR TASK**, **CRITICAL CONSTRAINTS**, **What you MUST/MUST NOT present**, **Foundation files**, **Novella scope**, **Major Events (IMMUTABLE)**. That’s the right spine for agent-driven generation.

### What’s strong
- The “IMMUTABLE” events and “MUST NOT” bans prevent accidental spoilers and deus ex nonsense.
- Per-node framing is tight; good handoffs and containment (“N09 only” style scope).

### Tighten this (so automation can’t wiggle)
- **Force a strict output schema.** Require YAML frontmatter with fixed keys:
  `node, title, logline, beats[1..7], must_include[], banned[], continuity_in[], continuity_out[], acceptance[]`. Agents love contracts; readers love consistency.
- **Add acceptance checks inline.** End each prompt with a tiny checklist:  
  “Contains 1 irreversible decision; names the cost; sets a timer; seeds 1 concrete image.” Makes it easy for a continuity pass to auto-fail garbage.
- **ID your “IMMUTABLE” events.** Give them stable IDs like `EVT-N09-01`. Then you can cross-reference in PR reviews and automated linters.
- **Name creation policy.** Explicitly forbid new proper nouns unless listed under `allowed_new_terms`. That’s how you strangle name drift in its crib.
- **Include a one-screen example output.** Not prose—just the schema filled. Models imitate patterns; give them the pattern.

If you want, I’ll whip up a tiny “Bible Linter” that asserts every prompt file contains the required sections/keys and fails a PR if anything’s missing. That’ll keep the prompt library as self-defending as the rest of the repo.

do that and give the explanation of what and why as i am handing these instruction to manus ai who can directly interact with the repo and push into it.

[ASSISTANT]
Yep—here’s a **drop-in Bible Prompt Linter** you can hand to Manus AI to add to the repo and wire into your existing guardrails. It validates each node’s prompt file, supports your current “legacy” prompt format, and **optionally** enforces the stricter YAML front-matter schema we talked about. Clear failures = blocked PRs. No vibes, just rules.

# Files to add

## 1) `.github/scripts/lint_bible_prompts.py`
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
OmniMeta Bible Prompt Linter

What it does (fast + ruthless):
- Finds all prompt files in 04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles matching N??_Prompt_*.(md|txt|yaml|yml)
- Passes if a file matches EITHER:
    A) New schema: YAML front-matter at top with required keys (see REQUIRED_* below)
    B) Legacy schema: required markdown headings (GENERATE, YOUR TASK, CRITICAL CONSTRAINTS, etc.)
- For N28/N29, enforces corrected titles (Echoes End / Apex of Stasis)
- For new schema, enforces:
    - beats length 3..7
    - acceptance includes: irreversible / cost / timer / image (keyword match)
    - node number matches filename
- Optional modes:
    --require-all       -> fail if any N01..N30 prompt is missing
    --strict-schema     -> require NEW YAML schema (legacy no longer accepted)
    --json              -> print machine-readable summary to stdout

Exit codes:
  0 = OK, 1 = failures detected
"""
import sys, re, json, argparse
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Tuple

PROMPT_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles")
PROMPT_PATTERNS = ("N??_Prompt_*.*",)
ALLOWED_EXTS = {".md", ".txt", ".yaml", ".yml"}

REQ_SCALARS = ["node", "title", "logline"]
REQ_LISTS   = ["beats", "must_include", "banned", "continuity_in", "continuity_out", "acceptance"]
ACCEPTANCE_KEYWORDS = ["irreversible", "cost", "timer", "image"]

TITLE_BY_NODE = {28: "Echoes End", 29: "Apex of Stasis"}

# ---- utils -----------------------------------------------------------------
def read_text(p: Path) -> str:
    try:
        return p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except Exception:
        return ""

def node_from_filename(name: str) -> int | None:
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Prompt_", name)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

def parse_frontmatter(text: str) -> Tuple[Dict[str, Any], str]:
    """
    Extremely simple front-matter parser supporting:
      key: value
      key:
        - item
        - item
    Returns (data_dict, body_without_frontmatter)
    """
    lines = text.splitlines()
    i = 0
    # skip leading blank
    while i < len(lines) and not lines[i].strip():
        i += 1
    if i >= len(lines) or lines[i].strip() != "---":
        return {}, text  # no frontmatter
    i += 1
    data: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    current_list_key: str | None = None
    while i < len(lines):
        ln = lines[i]
        if ln.strip() == "---":
            i += 1
            break
        # key: value
        m = re.match(r"^\s*([A-Za-z0-9_]+)\s*:\s*(.*)$", ln)
        if m:
            key, val = m.group(1), m.group(2).strip()
            if val == "" and key in REQ_LISTS:
                data[key] = []
                current_list_key = key
            else:
                data[key] = val
                current_list_key = key if key in REQ_LISTS else None
        else:
            # list item?
            m2 = re.match(r"^\s*-\s+(.*)$", ln)
            if m2 and current_list_key:
                data.setdefault(current_list_key, [])
                data[current_list_key].append(m2.group(1).strip())
        i += 1
    body = "\n".join(lines[i:])
    return data, body

def has_legacy_sections(text: str) -> List[str]:
    """Return list of missing legacy headings (empty if OK). Case-insensitive, flexible spacing."""
    patterns = {
        "GENERATE": r"^\s*#\s*GENERATE\b",
        "YOUR TASK": r"^\s*#\s*YOUR\s+TASK\b",
        "CRITICAL CONSTRAINTS": r"^\s*#\s*CRITICAL\s+CONSTRAINTS\b",
        "MUST PRESENT": r"^\s*#\s*WHAT\s+YOU\s+MUST\s+PRESENT\b",
        "MUST NOT": r"^\s*#\s*WHAT\s+YOU\s+MUST\s+NOT\s+PRESENT\b",
        "FOUNDATION": r"^\s*#\s*FOUNDATION\s+FILES.*",
        "NOVELLA SCOPE": r"^\s*#\s*NOVELLA\s+SCOPE\b",
        "IMMUTABLE": r"^\s*#\s*MAJOR\s+EVENTS\s*\(IMMUTABLE\)\b",
    }
    missing = []
    for label, pat in patterns.items():
        if not re.search(pat, text, flags=re.I | re.M):
            missing.append(label)
    return missing

def find_immutable_bullets(text: str) -> int:
    # count bullets under the IMMUTABLE section (rudimentary)
    m = re.search(r"^\s*#\s*MAJOR\s+EVENTS\s*\(IMMUTABLE\)\b(.*?)(?:^\s*#\s|\Z)", text, flags=re.I | re.M | re.S)
    if not m:
        return 0
    block = m.group(1)
    return len(re.findall(r"^\s*[-*]\s+", block, flags=re.M))

# ---- validators -------------------------------------------------------------
def validate_yaml_schema(front: Dict[str, Any], filename_node: int) -> List[str]:
    errs = []
    # required scalars
    for k in REQ_SCALARS:
        if k not in front or str(front[k]).strip() == "":
            errs.append(f"Missing YAML key: {k}")
    # required lists
    for k in REQ_LISTS:
        if k not in front or not isinstance(front[k], list) or len(front[k]) == 0:
            errs.append(f"Missing/empty YAML list: {k}")
    # node match
    try:
        n_val = front.get("node")
        node_num = int(str(n_val).replace("N", "").strip())
        if filename_node and node_num != filename_node:
            errs.append(f"Node mismatch: frontmatter says N{node_num:02d}, filename is N{filename_node:02d}")
    except Exception:
        errs.append("YAML 'node' must be an int or 'N##'")
    # beats length
    if "beats" in front:
        blen = len(front["beats"])
        if blen < 3 or blen > 7:
            errs.append(f"beats must contain 3..7 items (found {blen})")
    # acceptance includes key concepts
    if "acceptance" in front:
        acc = " ".join(front["acceptance"]).lower()
        for kw in ACCEPTANCE_KEYWORDS:
            if kw not in acc:
                errs.append(f"acceptance missing keyword: {kw}")
    # N28/N29 titles
    if filename_node in TITLE_BY_NODE:
        want = TITLE_BY_NODE[filename_node]
        got = str(front.get("title", "")).strip()
        if got != want:
            errs.append(f"N{filename_node:02d} title must be '{want}' (got '{got}')")
    return errs

def validate_legacy(text: str, filename_node: int) -> List[str]:
    errs = []
    missing = has_legacy_sections(text)
    if missing:
        errs.append("Missing legacy sections: " + ", ".join(missing))
    # IMMUTABLE should have >=1 bullet
    if find_immutable_bullets(text) == 0:
        errs.append("IMMUTABLE section has no bullet points")
    # N28/N29 title check (best-effort)
    if filename_node in (28, 29):
        # try to read the heading line after GENERATE for the quoted title
        m = re.search(r"^\s*#\s*GENERATE.*?—\s*\"([^\"]+)\"", text, flags=re.M)
        if m:
            got = m.group(1).strip()
            want = TITLE_BY_NODE[filename_node]
            if got != want:
                errs.append(f"N{filename_node:02d} title must be '{want}' (got '{got}')")
    return errs

# ---- main ------------------------------------------------------------------
def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--require-all", action="store_true", help="Require prompts for N01..N30 to exist")
    ap.add_argument("--strict-schema", action="store_true", help="Require YAML schema; do not accept legacy headings")
    ap.add_argument("--json", action="store_true", help="Print JSON summary")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    root = Path(".").resolve()
    prompt_root = (root / PROMPT_DIR)
    results = []

    # discover files
    files: List[Path] = []
    if prompt_root.exists():
        for pat in PROMPT_PATTERNS:
            files.extend(sorted([p for p in prompt_root.glob(pat) if p.suffix.lower() in ALLOWED_EXTS]))
    files = sorted(files, key=lambda p: p.name)

    # optional completeness check
    missing_nodes = []
    if args.require_all:
        present_nodes = {node_from_filename(p.name) for p in files if node_from_filename(p.name)}
        for i in range(1, 31):
            if i not in present_nodes:
                missing_nodes.append(i)

    failures = 0
    for p in files:
        text = read_text(p)
        fname_node = node_from_filename(p.name)
        front, body = parse_frontmatter(text)
        used_schema = False
        errs = []
        if front:
            used_schema = True
            errs = validate_yaml_schema(front, fname_node or -1)
        if not front or (errs and not args.strict_schema):
            # Try legacy if either no frontmatter OR invalid schema but not strict
            legacy_errs = validate_legacy(text, fname_node or -1)
            if not front or (errs and not args.strict_schema and not legacy_errs):
                # legacy accepted
                errs = []
                used_schema = False
            else:
                # choose the smaller error list to show
                if not args.strict_schema and len(legacy_errs) < len(errs):
                    errs = legacy_errs
                    used_schema = False
        results.append({
            "file": str(p.relative_to(root)),
            "node": fname_node,
            "used_schema": used_schema,
            "errors": errs
        })
        if errs:
            failures += 1

    if args.require_all and missing_nodes:
        failures += 1

    if args.json:
        print(json.dumps({
            "missing_nodes": [f"N{n:02d}" for n in missing_nodes],
            "results": results
        }, indent=2))
    else:
        if args.require_all and missing_nodes:
            print("❌ Missing prompt files for:", ", ".join(f"N{n:02d}" for n in missing_nodes))
        for r in results:
            if r["errors"]:
                print(f"❌ {r['file']} [{f'N{r['node']:02d}' if r['node'] else '?'}]:")
                for e in r["errors"]:
                    print(f"   - {e}")
            else:
                print(f"✅ {r['file']} [{f'N{r['node']:02d}' if r['node'] else '?'}] ({'YAML' if r['used_schema'] else 'legacy'})")

    sys.exit(1 if failures or (args.require_all and missing_nodes) else 0)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### Why this script (what it enforces + why it matters)
- **Two-lane runway:** passes **legacy** prompts today (so you don’t break the repo) *or* the **new YAML schema** (so you can upgrade piecemeal).  
- **N28/N29 title canon:** hard fail if titles drift. Because canon is sacred.  
- **Actionability:** the YAML lane forces `logline`, 3–7 `beats`, and an `acceptance` list containing **irreversible**, **cost**, **timer**, **image** keywords. If a prompt can’t yield those, automation produces mush.  
- **Determinism:** filename → node number → content node number must match, preventing misrouted runs.

```yaml
repos:
  - repo: local
    hooks:
      - id: omnimeta-prompt-lint
        name: omnimeta-prompt-lint
        entry: python3 .github/scripts/lint_bible_prompts.py --json
        language: system
        pass_filenames: false
```

> Why `--json`? pre-commit.ci shows structured output cleanly; failures still exit non-zero.

- `make lint-prompts-strict` → future switch: *only* YAML allowed and **all N01–N30** required.

# 1) Script: migrate legacy prompt files → YAML front-matter

**Path:** `.github/scripts/migrate_prompts_to_yaml.py`

**Why:** Converts your current `# GENERATE / YOUR TASK / CRITICAL CONSTRAINTS / MUST / MUST NOT / FOUNDATION / NOVELLA SCOPE / IMMUTABLE` format into the new schema your linter enforces. Keeps the original body, adds strict, machine-readable front-matter.

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Migrate legacy Bible prompt files to YAML front-matter.

- Parses headings from legacy prompts (md/txt) and builds front-matter:
  node, title, logline, beats, must_include, banned, continuity_in, continuity_out, acceptance
- Leaves the original content intact below the front-matter fence.
- Idempotent: run again and it won’t double-add front-matter.
- Best-effort extraction; leaves TODOs if a section is missing.

Usage:
  python3 .github/scripts/migrate_prompts_to_yaml.py [--write] [--nodes N01,N02,...]

Without --write it shows a preview diff in the console (non-destructive).
"""
import re, sys, argparse, difflib
from pathlib import Path

PROMPT_DIR = Path("04_Writer_Deliverables/02_Bibles")
GLOBS = ("N??_Prompt_*.*",)
EXTS = {".md", ".txt"}
TITLE_BY_NODE = {28: "Echoes End", 29: "Apex of Stasis"}

def read_text(p): 
    return p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")

def write_text(p, s): 
    p.write_text(s, encoding="utf-8")

def node_from_name(name):
    m = re.search(r"N(\d{2})_Prompt_", name)
    return int(m.group(1)) if m else None

def parse_legacy(text):
    # crude slicer for sections
    def section(head):
        pat = rf"^\s*#\s*{head}\b(.*?)(?=^\s*#\s|\Z)"
        m = re.search(pat, text, flags=re.I|re.M|re.S)
        return m.group(1).strip() if m else ""

    gen_line = re.search(r'^\s*#\s*GENERATE.*?—\s*"([^"]+)"', text, flags=re.M)
    title = gen_line.group(1).strip() if gen_line else ""

    your_task = section("YOUR\\s+TASK")
    constraints = section("CRITICAL\\s+CONSTRAINTS")
    must_present = section("WHAT\\s+YOU\\s+MUST\\s+PRESENT")
    must_not = section("WHAT\\s+YOU\\s+MUST\\s+NOT\\s+PRESENT")
    foundation = section("FOUNDATION\\s+FILES.*")
    novella = section("NOVELLA\\s+SCOPE")
    immutable = section("MAJOR\\s+EVENTS\\s*\\(IMMUTABLE\\)")

    # extract bullets into lists
    def bullets(block):
        return [re.sub(r'^\s*[-*]\s+', '', ln).strip()
                for ln in block.splitlines() if re.match(r'^\s*[-*]\s+', ln)]

    beats = bullets(novella) or bullets(your_task)
    must_include = bullets(must_present)
    banned = bullets(must_not)

    # continuity guessing: pull file references from foundation block
    continuity_in = re.findall(r'(N\d{2}_[A-Za-z0-9_]+\\.\w+)', foundation)
    # continuity out: try to infer from last lines of novella/must_present
    continuity_out = []

    acceptance = []
    # seed default acceptance if empty
    if not acceptance:
        acceptance = [
            "Includes one irreversible decision",
            "Names a concrete cost for success",
            "Establishes a timer/pressure element",
            "Contains at least one specific, visual image"
        ]

    return {
        "title": title,
        "logline": (your_task.splitlines() or ["TODO: fill logline from YOUR TASK"])[0].strip(),
        "beats": beats[:7],
        "must_include": must_include,
        "banned": banned,
        "continuity_in": continuity_in[:10],
        "continuity_out": continuity_out,
        "acceptance": acceptance
    }

def has_frontmatter(text): 
    return text.lstrip().startswith("---\n")

def build_frontmatter(node_num, data):
    # enforce canon titles on N28/N29
    if node_num in TITLE_BY_NODE and data["title"]:
        data["title"] = TITLE_BY_NODE[node_num]

    def list_block(key):
        items = data.get(key, [])
        if not items: return f"{key}: []"
        return f"{key}:\n" + "".join([f"  - {i}\n" for i in items])

    fm = [
        "---",
        f"node: {node_num}",
        f"title: {data.get('title','').strip() or 'TODO'}",
        f"logline: {data.get('logline','').strip() or 'TODO'}",
        list_block("beats"),
        list_block("must_include"),
        list_block("banned"),
        list_block("continuity_in"),
        list_block("continuity_out"),
        list_block("acceptance"),
        "---",
        ""
    ]
    return "\n".join(fm)

def migrate_file(p: Path, write=False):
    if p.suffix.lower() not in EXTS: 
        return None
    text = read_text(p)
    if has_frontmatter(text):
        return None  # already migrated

    node_num = node_from_name(p.name)
    legacy = parse_legacy(text)
    fm = build_frontmatter(node_num, legacy)
    new_text = fm + text
    if not write:
        diff = difflib.unified_diff(text.splitlines(), new_text.splitlines(),
                                    fromfile=p.name, tofile=p.name+" (migrated)", lineterm="")
        print("\n".join(diff))
    else:
        write_text(p, new_text)
    return True

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--write", action="store_true", help="Apply changes in-place")
    ap.add_argument("--nodes", type=str, help="Comma list like N01,N02,...")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    allow = None
    if args.nodes:
        allow = {int(n[1:]) for n in args.nodes.split(",")}

    targets = []
    for pat in GLOBS:
        for p in sorted((PROMPT_DIR).glob(pat)):
            if p.suffix.lower() in EXTS:
                if allow is None or node_from_name(p.name) in allow:
                    targets.append(p)

    changed = 0
    for p in targets:
        res = migrate_file(p, write=args.write)
        if res: changed += 1

    print(f"Processed {len(targets)} file(s); migrated: {changed}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

**How Manus should use it:**
```
# preview diffs for N01..N05 (no changes)
python3 .github/scripts/migrate_prompts_to_yaml.py --nodes N01,N02,N03,N04,N05

# apply
python3 .github/scripts/migrate_prompts_to_yaml.py --nodes N01,N02,N03,N04,N05 --write

# run linter in permissive mode (should pass)
make lint-prompts
```

When ≥90% are migrated, flip to strict:
```
make lint-prompts-strict   # this enforces YAML + all 30 present
```
